## Interaction Log

### System — 2026-07-01T18:46:40.250693

[Compressed Memory Summary]
The following is a compressed summary of earlier conversation turns, replacing the raw transcript to stay within the context window.

**Task:** Perform a full operational health check of the OWL swarm stack.

**Required actions:**
1. Call `blofin_get_stack_health` (no parameters) to obtain operational health snapshot (caches, feeds, errors, equity).
2. Call `blofin_get_swarm_learning_report` (no parameters) to retrieve the latest swarm learning report (what was learned, improved, fixed, with proof).
3. Combine the two results into a strict JSON object with the following fields:
   - `status`: overall health status (e.g., "healthy", "degraded", "critical").
   - `issues`: list of identified problems or anomalies.
   - `repair_actions`: recommended remediation steps for each issue.
   - `confidence`: confidence score (0‑1) for the assessment.
   - `narrative`: concise human‑readable summary explaining the findings.

**Constraints:** Output must be valid JSON matching the schema above; no extra text. No further function calls beyond the two specified.

### Key Issues & Immediate Actions
1. **Rate‑limit (HTTP 429) on balance endpoint** – the live account snapshot could not be fetched; the system fell back to a disk snapshot.  
   *Action:* Activate API‑cool‑down back‑off, use cached equity data, and schedule a retry after ~2 min.  

2. **Missing TP/SL on all open positions** – violates the mandatory rule.  
   *Action:* Immediately issue `blofin_place_tpsl` (or `blofin_ensure_position_tpsl`) for STABLE‑USDT, BAS‑USDT, and ADA‑USDT with sensible profit/stop levels.  

3. **Blocked symbols** – ADA‑USDT cannot receive new buys; STABLE‑USDT & BAS‑USDT cannot receive additional short adds.  
   *Action:* When selecting new trade candidates, exclude these IDs per the rules; consider other symbols from the 511‑symbol universe.  

4. **Log warning about empty live API** – indicates possible broader connectivity issues.  
   *Action:* Verify WebSocket connection health; if persistent, trigger a reconnection routine and alert the Ops monitor.
